<div class="col-a">
<div id="page-2847" class="elements-box post-2847 page type-page status-publish hentry">
<h5 style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #339966;">ဓမၼပါရဂူအရွင္ေဇာတိက(ေညာင္တုန္း)ဆရာေတာ္ ေဟာၾကားေတာ္မူေသာ တရားေတာ္မ်ား စုစည္းမွု (MP3)</span></h5>
<h5 style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #339966;"><span style="color: #ff9900;"><a href="https://www.thitsarparamisociety.com/ashin-zawtika-nyaungdone/" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ff9900;">ဓမၼပါရဂူအရွင္ေဇာတိက(ေညာင္တုန္း)ဆရာေတာ္ ေဟာၾကားေတာ္မူေသာ တရားေတာ္မ်ား စုစည္းမွု (MP4) Click</span></a></span><br>
</span></h5>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p><span style="color: #339966;"><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/10-1-2016/10-1-16-1.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၁။ စိတ္ေလွ်ာက္လမ္း တရားေတာ္ အပိုင္း (၁) (၁၀.၁.၂၀၁၆)ွ Singapore</span></a></span></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #339966;"><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/10-1-2016/10-1-16-2.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၂။ စိတ္ေလွ်ာက္လမ္း တရားေတာ္ အပိုင္း (၂) (၁၀.၁.၂၀၁၆) Singapore</span></a></span></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #339966;"><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/10-1-2016/10-1-16-3.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၃။ စိတ္ေလွ်ာက္လမ္း တရားေတာ္ အပိုင္း (၃) (၁၀.၁.၂၀၁၆) Singapore</span></a></span></span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p><span style="color: #339966;">သာမညဖလသုတၱန္ႏွင့္ သူေတာ္ေကာင္းမ်ား လိုက္နာက်င့္သံုးရမည့္ တရားေတာ္မ်ား<br>
</span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/1-1-2016-Singapore/1-1-2016-1.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၁။ တရားေတာ္ အပိုင္း-၁ (၁.၁.၂၀၁၆)</span></a></span></p>

<p><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/1-1-2016-Singapore/3-1-2016-4.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၁၄။ တရားေတာ္ အပိုင္း-၄ (၃.၁.၂၀၁၆)</span></span></a></p>
<p><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/1-1-2016-Singapore/3-1-2016-5.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၁၅။ တရားေတာ္ အပိုင္း-၅ (၃.၁.၂၀၁၆)</span></span></a></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p><span style="color: #339966;">လူေနမႈဘဝ အမွန္ရေစဖို႔ “အနတၱလကၡဏသုတ္” လက္ေတြ႕က်င့္စဥ္ သင္တန္း တရားေတာ္မ်ား (၇.၆.၂၀၁၅)</span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/anattalakkhaNa%287.6.2015%29/anatta1.mp3"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၁။ “အနတၱလကၡဏသုတ္” လက္ေတြ႕က်င့္စဥ္ (အပိုင္း – ၁)</span></a></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/anattalakkhaNa%287.6.2015%29/anatta2.mp3"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၂။ “အနတၱလကၡဏသုတ္” လက္ေတြ႕က်င့္စဥ္ (အပိုင္း – ၂)</span></a></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/anattalakkhaNa%287.6.2015%29/anatta3.mp3"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၃။ “အနတၱလကၡဏသုတ္” လက္ေတြ႕က်င့္စဥ္ (အပိုင္း – ၃)</span></a></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/anattalakkhaNa%287.6.2015%29/anatta4.mp3"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၄။ “အနတၱလကၡဏသုတ္” လက္ေတြ႕က်င့္စဥ္ (အပိုင္း – ၄)</span></a></span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p><span style="color: #339966;">(၂)ရက္တာ လက္ေတြက်င့္စဥ္ဓမၼစၾကာ သင္တန္းတရားေတာ္မ်ား (၃၁.၅.၂၀၁၅)မွ (၁.၆.၂၀၁၅)ထိ</span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/Dhammacakka/150531_001.MP3"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၁။ လက္ေတြ႕က်င့္စဥ္ ဓမၼစၾကာ သင္တန္း အပိုင္း(၁)</span></a></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/Dhammacakka/150531_002.MP3"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၂။ လက္ေတြ႕က်င့္စဥ္ ဓမၼစၾကာ သင္တန္း အပိုင္း(၂)</span></a></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/Dhammacakka/150531_003.MP3"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၃။ လက္ေတြ႕က်င့္စဥ္ ဓမၼစၾကာ သင္တန္း အပိုင္း(၃)</span></a></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/Dhammacakka/150531_004.MP3"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၄။ လက္ေတြ႕က်င့္စဥ္ ဓမၼစၾကာ သင္တန္း အပိုင္း(၄)</span></a></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/Dhammacakka/150601_001.MP3"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၅။ လက္ေတြ႕က်င့္စဥ္ ဓမၼစၾကာ သင္တန္း အပိုင္း(၅)</span></a></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/Dhammacakka/150601_002.MP3"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၆။ လက္ေတြ႕က်င့္စဥ္ ဓမၼစၾကာ သင္တန္း အပိုင္း(၆)</span></a></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/Dhammacakka/150601_003.MP3"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၇။ လက္ေတြ႕က်င့္စဥ္ ဓမၼစၾကာ သင္တန္း အပိုင္း(၇)</span></a></span></p>
<p><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/Dhammacakka/150601_004.MP3"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၈။ လက္ေတြ႕က်င့္စဥ္ ဓမၼစၾကာ သင္တန္း အပိုင္း(၈)</span></a><span style="color: #ffcc00;"> </span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/16.5.15.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">(၁၆.၅.၂၀၁၅) စေနေနေန႔ ညခ်မ္း (၇:၀၀) နာရီ တိုပါးရိုးျမန္မုဘုန္းေတာ္ႀကီးေက်ာင္းတြင္ ေဟာၾကားေတာ္မူေသာ ညီညြတ္ႏိုင္မွ ခ်မ္းသာရ တာားေတာ္</span></a></span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p><span style="color: #339966;">(၁၇.၅.၂၀၁၅) တနဂၤေႏြေန႔၊ သစၥာပါရမီမွ ႀကီးမွဴးက်င္းပေသာ (၂၄၂)ႀကိမ္ေျမာက္ တစ္ေန႔တာ အလုပ္ေပးတရားစခန္းတြင္ ေဟၾကားေတာ္မူခဲ့ေသာ တရားေတာ္မ်ား</span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/17-5-2015/150517_001.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၁။ ေန႔ခင္း (၁း၃၀)မွ (၂း၀၀)ထိ ေဟာၾကားေတာ္မူေသာ အလုပ္ေပးတရားေတာ္</span></a></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/17-5-2015/150517_002.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၂။ ေန႔ခင္း (၂း၃၀)မွ (၃း၃၀)ထိ ေဟာၾကားေတာ္မူေသာ အလုပ္ေပးတရားေတာ္</span></a></span></p>
<p><span style="text-decoration: underline; color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/17-5-2015/150517_003.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00; text-decoration: underline;">၃။ ေန႔ခင္း (၅း၀၀)မွ (၆း၀၀)ထိ ေဟာၾကားေတာ္မူေသာ အလုပ္ေပးတရားေတာ္</span></a></span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p><span style="color: #339966;">(၁.၅.၂၀၁၅) မွ (၃.၅.၂၀၁၅) ေန႔အထိ သစၥာပါရမီ ဓမၼရိပ္သာ (စင္ကာပူ)မွ ႀကီးမွဴးက်င္းပခဲ့ေသာ “ရာဟုေလာဝါဒသုတၱန္ သင္တန္း” တရားေတာ္မ်ား</span></p>

<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/YarHuLawWarDa/YarHuLawWaDa-Day1-P2.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၂။ သင္တန္း ပထမေန႔ (ဒုတိယပိုင္း)</span></a></span></p>

<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/YarHuLawWarDa/YarHuLawWaDa-Day2-P2.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၂။ သင္တန္း ဒုတိယေန႔ (ဒုတိယပိုင္း)</span></a></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/YarHuLawWarDa/YarHuLawWaDa-Day2-P3.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၃။ သင္တန္း ဒုတိယေန႔ (တတိယပိုင္း)</span></a></span></p>

<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/YarHuLawWarDa/YarHuLawWaDa-Day3-P2.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၂။ သင္တန္း တတိယေန႔ (ဒုတိယပိုင္း)</span></a></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/YarHuLawWarDa/YarHuLawWaDa-Day3-P3.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၃။ သင္တန္း တတိယေန႔ (တတိယပိုင္း)</span></a></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/YarHuLawWarDa/YarHuLawWaDa-Day3-P4.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၄။ သင္တန္း တတိယေန႔ (စတုတၳပိုင္း)</span></a></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/YarHuLawWarDa/YarHuLawWaDa-Day3-Q&amp;A.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၅။ သင္တန္း တတိယေန႔ (အေမးအေျဖ)</span></a></span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/2015/150101_001.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၁။ (၁.၁.၂၀၁၅)ေန႔ “ႏွစ္ဦးမဂၤလာ အႏၱရာယ္ကင္း ပရိတ္ရြတ္ဖတ္ပူေဇာ္ပြဲႏွင့္ ကေလးလူႀကီး ဓမၼသဘင္” တြင္ ေဟာၾကားေတာ္မူခဲ့ေသာ ကေလးငယ္မ်ားအတြက္ တရားေတာ္</span></a></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/2015/150101_003.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၂။ (၁.၁.၂၀၁၅)ေန႔ “ႏွစ္ဦးမဂၤလာ အႏၱရာယ္ကင္း ပရိတ္ရြတ္ဖတ္ပူေဇာ္ပြဲႏွင့္ ကေလးလူႀကီး ဓမၼသဘင္” တြင္ ေဟာၾကားေတာ္မူခဲ့ေသာ “လူမွန္ေနရာမွန္ တရားေတာ္”</span></a></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #339966;">(၂၂၄)ႀကိမ္ေျမာက္ တစ္ေန႔တာ မိုးကုတ္ဝိပႆနာ အလုပ္ေပးတရားစခန္း ဓမၼဒါနအထိမ္းအမွတ္ (၂၅.၁၂.၂၀၁၄)ေန႔မွ (၂၆.၁၂.၂၀၁၄)ေန႔အထိ “ခ်က္ခ်င္းလက္ငင္းသံုး ဗုဒၶအဘိဓမၼာသင္တန္း” တရားေတာ္မ်ား</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/224times-meditation/25.12.2014/Part1%2825.12.2014%29.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၁။ ခ်က္ခ်င္းလက္ငင္းသုံးဗုဒၶအဘိဓမၼာသင္တန္း ပထမေန႔ (အပိုင္း – ၁) (၂၅.၁၂.၂၀၁၄) (၁၀း၀၀)နာရီမွ (၁၁း၁၅)နာရီ</span></a></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/224times-meditation/25.12.2014/part2%2825.12.2014%29.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၂။ ခ်က္ခ်င္းလက္ငင္းသုံးဗုဒၶအဘိဓမၼာသင္တန္း ပထမေန႔ (အပိုင္း – ၂) (၂၅.၁၂.၂၀၁၄) (၁၂း၃၀)နာရီမွ (၁၃း၃၀)နာရီ</span></a></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/224times-meditation/25.12.2014/part3%2825.12.2014%29.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၃။ ခ်က္ခ်င္းလက္ငင္းသုံးဗုဒၶအဘိဓမၼာသင္တန္း ပထမေန႔ (အပိုင္း – ၃) (၂၅.၁၂.၂၀၁၄) (၁၄း၀၀)နာရီမွ (၁၅း၀၀)နာရီ</span></a></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/224times-meditation/25.12.2014/Part4%2825.12.2014%29.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၄။ ခ်က္ခ်င္းလက္ငင္းသုံးဗုဒၶအဘိဓမၼာသင္တန္း ပထမေန႔ (အပိုင္း – ၄) (၂၅.၁၂.၂၀၁၄) (၁၅း၃၀)နာရီမွ (၁၆း၃၀)နာရီ</span></a></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/224times-meditation/25.12.2014/Q&amp;A%2825.12.2014%29.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၅။ ခ်က္ခ်င္းလက္ငင္းသုံးဗုဒၶအဘိဓမၼာသင္တန္း ပထမေန႔ (အေမးအေျဖ) (၂၅.၁၂.၂၀၁၄) (၁၇း၀၀)နာရီမွ (၁၈း၀၀)နာရီ</span></a></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"> </span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a title="ခ်က္ခ်င္းလက္ငင္းသံုး အဘိဓမၼာ ဒုတိယေန႔ ပထမပိုင္း" href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/224times-meditation/26.12.2014/Part1%2826.12.2014%29.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၆။ ခ်က္ခ်င္းလက္ငင္းသုံးဗုဒၶအဘိဓမၼာသင္တန္း ဒုတိယေန႔ (အပိုင္း – ၁) (၂၆.၁၂.၂၀၁၄) (၁၄း၃၀)နာရီမွ (၁၅း၁၅)နာရီ</span></a></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a title="ခ်က္ခ်င္းလက္ငင္းသံုး အဘိဓမၼာ ဒုတိယေန႔ ဒုတိယပိုင္း" href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/224times-meditation/32kb/Part2%2826.12.2014%29.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၇။ ခ်က္ခ်င္းလက္ငင္းသုံးဗုဒၶအဘိဓမၼာသင္တန္း ဒုတိယေန႔ (အပိုင္း – ၂) (၂၆.၁၂.၂၀၁၄) (၁၅း၃၀)နာရီမွ (၁၆း၃၀)နာရီ</span></a></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a title="ခ်က္ခ်င္းလက္ငင္းသံုး အဘိဓမၼာ တတိယေန႔ (အေမး/အေျဖ)" href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/224times-meditation/32kb/Q&amp;A%20day2.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၈။ ခ်က္ခ်င္းလက္ငင္းသုံးဗုဒၶအဘိဓမၼာသင္တန္း ဒုတိယေန႔ (အပိုင္း – ၃) (၂၆.၁၂.၂၀၁၄) (၁၇း၀၀)နာရီမွ (၁၈း၀၀)နာရီ</span></a></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"> </span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a title="ခ်က္ခ်င္းလက္ငင္းသံုး အဘိဓမၼာ တတိယေန႔ ပထမပိုင္း" href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/224times-meditation/27.12.2014/27.12.14%20P1.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၉။ ခ်က္ခ်င္းလက္ငင္းသုံးဗုဒၶအဘိဓမၼာသင္တန္း တတိယေန႔ (အပိုင္း – ၁) (၂၇.၁၂.၂၀၁၄) (၁၀း၀၀)နာရီမွ (၁၁း၁၅)နာရီ</span></a></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a title="ခ်က္ခ်င္းလက္ငင္းသံုး အဘိဓမၼာ တတိယေန႔ ဒုတိယပိုင္း" href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/224times-meditation/27.12.2014/27.12.14P2.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၁၀။ ခ်က္ခ်င္းလက္ငင္းသုံးဗုဒၶအဘိဓမၼာသင္တန္း တတိယေန႔ (အပိုင္း – ၂) (၂၇.၁၂.၂၀၁၄) (၁၂း၃၀)နာရီမွ (၁၃း၃၀)နာရီ</span></a></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a title="ခ်က္ခ်င္းလက္ငင္းသံုး အဘိဓမၼာ တတိယေန႔ တတိယပိုင္း" href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/224times-meditation/27.12.2014/27.12.14P3.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၁၁။ ခ်က္ခ်င္းလက္ငင္းသုံးဗုဒၶအဘိဓမၼာသင္တန္း တတိယေန႔ (အပိုင္း – ၃) (၂၇.၁၂.၂၀၁၄) (၁၄း၀၀)နာရီမွ (၁၅း၀၀)နာရီ</span></a></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a title="ခ်က္ခ်င္းလက္ငင္းသံုး အဘိဓမၼာ တတိယေန႔ စတုတၳပိုင္း" href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/224times-meditation/27.12.2014/27.12.14P4.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၁၂။ ခ်က္ခ်င္းလက္ငင္းသုံးဗုဒၶအဘိဓမၼာသင္တန္း တတိယေန႔ (အပိုင္း – ၄) (၂၇.၁၂.၂၀၁၄) (၁၅း၃၀)နာရီမွ (၁၆း၃၀)နာရီ</span></a></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a title="ခ်က္ခ်င္းလက္ငင္းသံုး အဘိဓမၼာ တတိယေန႔ (အေမး/အေျဖ)" href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/224times-meditation/27.12.2014/27.12.14Q&amp;A.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၁၃။ ခ်က္ခ်င္းလက္ငင္းသုံးဗုဒၶအဘိဓမၼာသင္တန္း တတိယေန႔ (အေမးအေျဖ) (၂၇.၁၂.၂၀၁၄) (၁၇း၀၀)နာရီမွ (၁၈း၀၀)နာရီ</span></a></span></p>

<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a title="အရိုင္းအယဥ္တရားေတာ္" href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/%2820.12.2014%29ToaPahyo.mp3"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၃။ အရိုင္း အယဥ္ တရားေတာ္ (၂၀.၁၂.၂၀၁၄)(၇း၀၀) တိုပါးရိုးဘုန္းေတာ္ႀကီးေက်ာင္း စင္ကာပူ</span></a></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/thitsarparami/223%201030.MP3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၄။ (၂၂၃)ႀကိမ္ေျမာက္ သစၥာပါရမီ တစ္ေန႔တာ အလုပ္ေပးတရားစခန္း နံနက္ခင္း (၁၀း၃၀)နာရီတြင္ ေဟာၾကားေတာ္မူေသာ တရားေတာ္ (၂၁.၁၂.၂၀၁၄)</span></a></span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/thitsarparami/223%20morning.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၅။ (၂၂၃)ႀကိမ္ေျမာက္ သစၥာပါရမီ တစ္ေန႔တာ အလုပ္ေပးတရားစခန္း ေန႔ခင္း (၁၂း၃၀)နာရီတြင္ ေဟာၾကားေတာ္မူေသာ တရားေတာ္ (၂၁.၁၂.၂၀၁၄)</span></a></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20%28Nyaung%20Done%29/thitsarparami/223%20afternoon.mp3" target="_blank"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၆။ (၂၂၃)ႀကိမ္ေျမာက္ သစၥာပါရမီ တစ္ေန႔တာ အလုပ္ေပးတရားစခန္း ညေနခင္း (၅း၀၀)နာရီတြင္ ေဟာၾကားေတာ္မူေသာ တရားေတာ္ (၂၁.၁၂.၂၀၁၄)</span></a></span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #339966;">စင္ကာပူႏိုင္ငံ၊ သစၥာပါရမီဓမၼရိပ္သာမွ ႀကီးမွဴးက်င္းပေသာ (၂၀၃)ႀကိမ္ေျမာက္ တစ္ေန႔တာ ဝိပႆ နာ အလုပ္ေပး တရားစခန္း ဓမၼဒါန ( ၃ ) ရက္တာ အပါယ္တံခါးပိတ္ ဝိသုဒၶိမဂ္ (က်င့္စဥ္) သင္တန္း တရားေတာ္မ်ား</span></p>
<p style="text-align: left;"><span style="color: #339966;"> (၂၆.၇.၂၀၁၄) မွ (၂၈.၇.၂၀၁၄) Japanese Garden Guest House Hall</span></p>

<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p><span style="color: #339966;">“ဓမၼပဒ သဘာဝ သင္တန္း တရားေတာ္မ်ား”</span></p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>

<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20(Nyaung%20Done)/dhammapada/20110504.mp3"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၂။ “ဓမၼပဒ သဘာဝ သင္တန္း တရားေတာ္” ယမကဝဂ္ ၊ ပ႒ကု႑လိဝတၳဳ (၄.၅.၂၀၁၁)</span></a></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20(Nyaung%20Done)/dhammapada/20110510.mp3"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၃။ “ဓမၼပဒ သဘာဝ သင္တန္း တရားေတာ္” ယမကဝဂ္ ၊ စူ႒ကာလ မဟာကာ႒ဝတၳဳ (၁၀.၅.၂၀၁၁)</span></a></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20(Nyaung%20Done)/dhammapada/20110511.mp3"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၄။ “ဓမၼပဒ သဘာဝ သင္တန္း တရားေတာ္” စိတၱဝဂ္ ၊ ေသာေယ်တၳရဝတၳဳ (၁၁.၅.၂၀၁၁)</span></a></span></p>

<p><span style="color: #ffcc00;"><a href="https://media.thitsarparamisociety.com/mp3/Sayardaw%20U%20Zawti%20Ka%20(Nyaung%20Done)/dhammapada/20110524.mp3"><span style="color: #ffcc00;">၆။ “ဓမၼပဒ သဘာဝ သင္တန္း တရားေတာ္” စိတၱဝဂ္ ၊ စိတၱဟတၳေထယ်ဝတၳဳ (၂၄.၅.၂၀၁၁)</span></a></span></p>

<div id="text-17" class="widget widget_text"><h3 class="widget-title">Feed Back</h3> <div class="textwidget"><p align="justify">ဓမၼမိတ္ေဆြ အေပါင္းတို ့ မိမိတုိ ့၏ တရားစခန္း အခက္အခဲမ်ား၊ နာၾကား အၾကံျပဳ လိုေသာ တရားဓမၼမ်ား ၊ ေမးျမန္းလိုေသာ ဓမၼေမးခြန္းမ်ား ၊ website ၾကည့္ရွုနာၾကားရာ ၌ အခက္အခဲမ်ား ျဖစ္ေပၚပါက ေအာက္ပါ Form တြင္ ျဖည့္စြက္၍ ေပးပို႔ အႀကံျပဳၾကပါရန္ ေမတၱာရပ္ခံအပ္ပါသည္။</p>

<script type="text/javascript">
		jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
			
		jQuery("#preloader-fopwcm").fadeOut(1500, function () {
			jQuery("#ecf-form-fopwcm").fadeIn(300);
			});
			
			$( '.ladda-button' ).ladda( 'bind' );

			$(function() {
				
						
				// Validation
				$("#form-fopwcm").validate(
				{					
					// Rules for form validation
					rules:
					{
					name0:{required: true},email1:{required: true,email: true},message2:{required: true,minlength: 10},
							
									
					},
										
					// Messages for form validation
					messages:
					{
					name0:{required: "This field is required"},email1:{required: "This field is required"},message2:{required: "This field is required"}					},					
					// Do not change code below
					errorPlacement: function(error, element) {
						error.insertAfter(element.parent());
						},
						
					submitHandler: function (form) {
										 ecf_onsubmit(jQuery('.form-fopwcm'));
						 
						 						 
						 },
						 
					invalidHandler: function (form) {	
					  	$.ladda( 'stopAll' );
					 	},
						 
					onkeyup: false,
					onfocusout: false,
					onclick: false
					
				});
			});	
			
			
			/* Form Submit ( Ajax ) */
			function ecf_onsubmit(form){	

				if(form.attr('action')=='#'){
					
					data = {};
					eldat = [];
					data['action'] = 'ecf_deliver_mail';
					data['formid'] = '12786';
					data['security'] = 'bfc69e80a1';
		
		
						
					jQuery('input, textarea', form).each(function(key){
						
						items = {};
						
						if (typeof $(this).data('type') === 'undefined') { return true; }
						

						
						items['type'] = $(this).data('type');
						items['label'] = $(this).data('label');
						items['value'] = this.value;
						items['name'] = this.name;

						eldat.push(items);
							
						}); // END  form).each(function(key){
							

													

						data['allelmnt'] = JSON.stringify(eldat);

						submitForm();
				
					return false;
					
				} // End if(form.attr('action')=='#'){
				
			} // End ecf_onsubmit 
			
			// Start submitForm		
			  function submitForm() {
				  
				jQuery.ajax({
					url: 'https://www.thitsarparamisociety.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php', 
					type: 'POST',
					dataType: 'json',
					data: data, 
					success: function(data) {
				
						if(data.Ok==true) {
									// success
							$("#form-fopwcm").get(0).reset();	
								
							if(data.msg == 'redirect') {
								window.location = "http://";
								} else {
									notifyme('Your Message Submitted Successfully', 'n', 'success', 'left middle');
									}
		
							}
							else {
								$("#form-fopwcm").get(0).reset();
								notifyme(data.msg, 'n', 'error', 'left middle');
								}
								
							$.ladda( 'stopAll' );	
									
							}
						});
						
										
					} // End submitForm
	
					
			// Notify	
			  function notifyme(msg, b, typ, pos) {
				  if (b == 'n') {
					  b = 'cf-submittedfopwcm';
				  } else {
					 b = 'atcfopwcm';
				  }
				  
				  $("#"+b).gnotify(msg,{
					  style: "nbootstrap",
					  elementPosition: pos,
					  className: typ
					  });
					  
					  msg = null;
					  typ = null;
					  
					}

		});		
		</script>
